Empty SMILES vs Name\n- Mentions missing SMILES entirely: 11559\n- Mentions missing Names entirely: 0\n\n## 4. Conclusion on `compare_catalysts` tool\nWithout a normalization lookup table, comparing catalysts by string-matching their `name` or `smiles` directly from the JSON array will be **misleading**.\nA catalyst like 'Pd/C' might appear under several name variants or missing SMILES strings. We recommend building a `catalyst_normalization` table in DuckDB to collapse synonyms to a canonical identifier before implementing a public-facing comparison tool.\n
